<div class=WordSection1>

<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='margin-top:0cm;margin-right:0cm;
margin-bottom:5.15pt;margin-left:12.0pt;text-align:center'><font size=2

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:0cm;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:0cm;

<h1 style='margin-left:-.25pt'><b><font size=6 color=black face=Calibri><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:22.0pt;line-height:141%;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif";
font-weight:bold'>1.</span></font></b><b><font face=Arial><span lang=EN-US
style='font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";font-weight:bold'> </span></font></b><font
face=宋体><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:KaiTi;mso-hansi-font-family:
KaiTi'>物理接口</span></font><b><font face=Calibri><span style='font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif";
font-weight:bold'> </span></font></b></h1>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:0cm;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:7.0pt;
margin-left:12.0pt;text-indent:24.0pt;line-height:110%'><font size=3
color=black face=宋体><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:110%;font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:KaiTi;mso-hansi-font-family:KaiTi'>车道计算机与称重设备之间的通讯连接方式为</span></font><font
size=3 face=KaiTi><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:110%;font-family:
KaiTi'> </span></font><font size=3><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
line-height:110%'>RS232 </span></font><font size=3 face=宋体><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:110%;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
KaiTi;mso-hansi-font-family:KaiTi'>串行连接，并采用异步全双工方式</span></font><font size=3><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:110%'>: </span></font></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:0cm;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:4.9pt;
margin-left:35.75pt;text-indent:-.5pt'><font size=3 color=black
face="Times New Roman"><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:
106%;font-family:"Times New Roman","serif"'>-</span></font><font size=3
face=Arial><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:106%;
font-family:"Arial","sans-serif"'> </span></font><font size=3><span lang=EN-US

  mso-hansi-font-family:KaiTi'>重新发送上一次的信息</span></font><font size=3><span

  </td>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:0cm;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:5.9pt;

宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:KaiTi;mso-hansi-font-family:KaiTi'>此信息由称重系统在收到命令</span></font><font
size=3 face=KaiTi><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:110%;font-family:
KaiTi'> </span></font><font size=3><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
line-height:110%'>3 </span></font><font size=3 face=宋体><span style='font-size:
12.0pt;line-height:110%;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:KaiTi;mso-hansi-font-family:
KaiTi'>后发送。</span></font><font size=3><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:
110%'> </span></font></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:6.65pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:
inter-ideograph;text-indent:24.0pt;line-height:103%'><font size=3 color=black
face=宋体><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:103%;font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:KaiTi;mso-hansi-font-family:KaiTi'>无论称重系统缓存是否存在数据，此信息</span></font><font
size=3><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:103%'>(</span></font><font
size=3 face=宋体><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:103%;font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:KaiTi;mso-hansi-font-family:KaiTi'>信息长度为</span></font><font
size=3 face=KaiTi><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:103%;font-family:
KaiTi'> </span></font><font size=3><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
line-height:103%'>18)</span></font><font size=3 face=宋体><span style='font-size:
12.0pt;line-height:103%;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:KaiTi;mso-hansi-font-family:
KaiTi'>包含的是当前处理车辆的轴重，如果车辆已经被检测完毕，缓存含有车辆信息，当前车辆的临时数据为空。</span></font><font
size=3><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:103%'> </span></font></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:4.25pt;text-indent:24.0pt;line-height:
110%'><font size=3 color=black face=宋体><span style='font-size:12.0pt;
line-height:110%;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:KaiTi;mso-hansi-font-family:
KaiTi'>在车辆倒车的时候，车轴数可以为负数，但重量和轴型和轴距不包含在此信息中</span></font><font size=3><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:110%'>(</span></font><font
size=3 face=宋体><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:110%;font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:KaiTi;mso-hansi-font-family:KaiTi'>信息长度为</span></font><font
size=3 face=KaiTi><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:110%;font-family:
KaiTi'> </span></font><font size=3><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
line-height:110%'>18)</span></font><font size=3 face=宋体><span style='font-size:
12.0pt;line-height:110%;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:KaiTi;mso-hansi-font-family:
KaiTi'>。仅在轴数为正数的时候才包含重量和轴型和轴距注意，上位机应先检测临时数据，知道临时数据为空，然后发</span></font><font
size=3 face=KaiTi><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:110%;font-family:
KaiTi'> </span></font><font size=3><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
line-height:110%'>1 </span></font><font size=3 face=宋体><span style='font-size:
12.0pt;line-height:110%;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:KaiTi;mso-hansi-font-family:
KaiTi'>命令，取整车数据</span></font><font size=3><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:
12.0pt;line-height:110%'>. </span></font></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:0cm;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:4.8pt;
margin-left:12.0pt;text-indent:24.0pt;line-height:110%'><font size=3

size=3 face=KaiTi><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:110%;font-family:
KaiTi'> </span></font><font size=3><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
line-height:110%'>15 </span></font><font size=3 face=宋体><span style='font-size:
12.0pt;line-height:110%;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:KaiTi;mso-hansi-font-family:
KaiTi'>个轴，则临时数据包含当前第</span></font><font size=3 face=KaiTi><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:110%;font-family:KaiTi'> </span></font><font
size=3><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:110%'>n </span></font><font
size=3 face=宋体><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:110%;font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:KaiTi;mso-hansi-font-family:KaiTi'>个包的数据，不再包含</span></font><font
size=3 face=KaiTi><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:110%;font-family:
KaiTi'> </span></font><font size=3><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
line-height:110%'>n*15 </span></font><font size=3 face=宋体><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:110%;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
KaiTi;mso-hansi-font-family:KaiTi'>个轴的数据</span></font><font size=3><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:110%'> </span></font></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:0cm;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:4.8pt;
margin-left:36.0pt'><font size=3 color=blue face=宋体><span style='font-size:
12.0pt;line-height:106%;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;

<h3 style='margin-top:0cm;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:22.75pt;margin-left:
-.25pt'><b><font size=5 color=black face=Calibri><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:16.0pt;line-height:110%'>2.2.7</span></font></b><font
face=Arial><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:"Arial","sans-serif"'> </span></font><font

<h1 style='margin-top:0cm;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:51.65pt;margin-left:
0cm;text-indent:0cm;line-height:106%'><b><font size=6 color=black face=Calibri><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:22.0pt;line-height:106%;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif";
font-weight:bold'>3.</span></font></b><b><font face=Arial><span lang=EN-US
style='font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";font-weight:bold'> </span></font></b><font
face=宋体><span style='font-family:宋体'>细节</span></font><b><font face=Calibri><span
style='font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif";font-weight:bold'> </span></font></b></h1>

<h2 style='margin-top:0cm;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:23.7pt;margin-left:
-.25pt'><font size=5 color=black face=Calibri><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:16.0pt;line-height:110%'>3.1</span></font><b><font face=Arial><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";font-weight:bold'> </span></font></b><font
face=宋体><span style='font-family:宋体'>原则</span></font> </h2>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:0cm;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:.25pt;
margin-left:35.25pt;text-indent:24.0pt;line-height:110%'><font size=3
color=black face=Calibri><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:
110%'>1.</span></font><font size=1 face="Times New Roman"><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:7.0pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Times New Roman","serif"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></font><font size=3 face=宋体><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:
110%;font-family:宋体'>协</span></font><font size=3 face=宋体><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:110%;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
KaiTi;mso-hansi-font-family:KaiTi'>议当中，</span></font><font size=3 face=Tahoma><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Tahoma","sans-serif"'>2
</span></font><font size=3 face=宋体><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:
110%;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:KaiTi;mso-hansi-font-family:KaiTi'>字节及</span></font><font
size=3 face=KaiTi><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:110%;font-family:
KaiTi'> </span></font><font size=3 face=Tahoma><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Tahoma","sans-serif"'>2 </span></font><font
size=3 face=宋体><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:110%;font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:KaiTi;mso-hansi-font-family:KaiTi'>字节以上的数据结构均为高位在前低位在后；</span></font><font
size=3><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:110%'> </span></font></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:0cm;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:.25pt;
margin-left:35.25pt;text-indent:24.0pt;line-height:110%'><font size=3
color=black face=Calibri><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:
110%'>2.</span></font><font size=1 face="Times New Roman"><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:7.0pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Times New Roman","serif"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></font><font size=3 face=宋体><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:
110%;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:KaiTi;mso-hansi-font-family:KaiTi'>在传输数据的过程中</span></font><font
size=3><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:110%'>,</span></font><font
size=3 face=宋体><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:110%;font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:KaiTi;mso-hansi-font-family:KaiTi'>如果此时收到信息</span></font><font
size=3><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:110%'>,</span></font><font
size=3 face=宋体><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:110%;font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:KaiTi;mso-hansi-font-family:KaiTi'>不能影响当前的数据传输；</span></font><font
size=3><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:110%'> </span></font></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:0cm;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:.25pt;
margin-left:35.25pt;text-indent:24.0pt;line-height:110%'><font size=3
color=black face=Calibri><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:
110%'>3.</span></font><font size=1 face="Times New Roman"><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:7.0pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Times New Roman","serif"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></font><font size=3 face=宋体><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:
110%;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:KaiTi;mso-hansi-font-family:KaiTi'>两个字节信息之间的时间间隔不能大于</span></font><font
size=3 face=KaiTi><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:110%;font-family:
KaiTi'> </span></font><font size=3><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
line-height:110%'>20ms,</span></font><font size=3 face=宋体><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:110%;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
KaiTi;mso-hansi-font-family:KaiTi'>否则此信息无法被正确接收；</span></font><font size=3><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:110%'> </span></font></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:0cm;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:.25pt;
margin-left:35.25pt;text-indent:24.0pt;line-height:110%'><font size=3
color=black face=Calibri><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:
110%'>4.</span></font><font size=1 face="Times New Roman"><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:7.0pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Times New Roman","serif"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></font><font size=3 face=宋体><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:
110%;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:KaiTi;mso-hansi-font-family:KaiTi'>称重系统和车道计算机发送的两个不同信息</span></font><font
size=3><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:110%'>,</span></font><font
size=3 face=宋体><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:110%;font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:KaiTi;mso-hansi-font-family:KaiTi'>最短时间间隔为</span></font><font
size=3 face=KaiTi><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:110%;font-family:
KaiTi'> </span></font><font size=3><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
line-height:110%'>50ms</span></font><font size=3 face=宋体><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:110%;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
KaiTi;mso-hansi-font-family:KaiTi'>；</span></font><font size=3><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:110%'> </span></font></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:0cm;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:.25pt;
margin-left:35.25pt;text-indent:24.0pt;line-height:110%'><font size=3
color=black face=Calibri><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:
110%'>5.</span></font><font size=1 face="Times New Roman"><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:7.0pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Times New Roman","serif"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></font><font size=3 face=宋体><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:
110%;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:KaiTi;mso-hansi-font-family:KaiTi'>在收到命令最后一个字节后必须在</span></font><font
size=3 face=KaiTi><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:110%;font-family:
KaiTi'> </span></font><font size=3><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
line-height:110%'>250ms </span></font><font size=3 face=宋体><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:110%;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
KaiTi;mso-hansi-font-family:KaiTi'>内应答</span></font><font size=3><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:110%'>,</span></font><font
size=3 face=宋体><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:110%;font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:KaiTi;mso-hansi-font-family:KaiTi'>否则就被认为该信息丢失并再次传送该命令</span></font><font
size=3><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:110%'>,</span></font><font
size=3 face=宋体><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:110%;font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:KaiTi;mso-hansi-font-family:KaiTi'>没有最短响应时间限制；</span></font><font
size=3><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:110%'> </span></font></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:0cm;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:.25pt;
margin-left:35.25pt;text-indent:24.0pt;line-height:110%'><font size=3
color=black face=Calibri><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:
110%'>6.</span></font><font size=1 face="Times New Roman"><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:7.0pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Times New Roman","serif"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></font><font size=3 face=宋体><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:
110%;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:KaiTi;mso-hansi-font-family:KaiTi'>对于车道计算机发出的所有命令，称重系统都必须应答；</span></font><font
size=3><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:110%'> </span></font></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:0cm;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:.25pt;
margin-left:35.25pt;text-indent:24.0pt;line-height:110%'><font size=3
color=black face=Calibri><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:
110%'>7.</span></font><font size=1 face="Times New Roman"><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:7.0pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Times New Roman","serif"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></font><font size=3 face=宋体><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:
110%;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:KaiTi;mso-hansi-font-family:KaiTi'>如果</span></font><font
size=3 face=KaiTi><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:110%;font-family:
KaiTi'> </span></font><font size=3><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
line-height:110%'>CRC </span></font><font size=3 face=宋体><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:110%;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
KaiTi;mso-hansi-font-family:KaiTi'>校验错误，则此信息会被理解为损坏且不会产生任何影响，车道计算机会重新发送命令。</span></font><font
size=3><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:110%'> </span></font></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:0cm;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:0cm;
margin-left:36.0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt'><font size=3 color=black face=宋体><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:106%;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>　</span></font><font size=3><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:106%'> </span></font><font size=3 face=宋体><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:106%;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>　</span></font></p>
